<type>file</type>
<content>
1: """Naive grouped GEMM + fused SwiGLU reference (correctness only, NOT the SOTA).
2: 
3: This is the up-projection of an MoE FFN. Each token i is assigned to K experts;
4: expert_indices[i*K + j] tells you which expert. Tokens are dispatched to experts
5: according to routing metadata; we compute, per expert e:
6: 
7:     h_e = silu(x_e @ W_gate[e])  *  (x_e @ W_up[e])
8: 
9: where x_e is the slice of permuted hidden states routed to expert e, with
10: expert_offsets[e]:expert_offsets[e+1] giving its row range in the permuted layout.
11: 
12: The reference loops over experts in Python. Slow, but pedagogically clear and
13: correct. Forbidden ops (torch.matmul, torch.bmm, F.linear, sonic_moe imports)
14: are NOT used here, but the reference is exempt — only solution.py is checked.
15: """
16: from __future__ import annotations
17: 
18: import torch
19: import torch.nn as nn
20: import torch.nn.functional as F

<type>file</type>
<content>
1: name: 06_sonic_moe_swiglu
2: display_name: "Sonic-MoE up-projection (Grouped GEMM + SwiGLU)"
3: precision: bf16
4: regime: compute
5: hardware: [RTX_PRO_6000]
6: peak_tflops_key: bf16
7: peak_bandwidth_key: dram
8: 
9: # Dense-equivalent FLOPs: gate GEMM + up GEMM + SwiGLU (negligible elementwise).
10: # Per token: 2*H*I FMAs for gate, 2*H*I for up => 2 * T_total * H * (2*I).
11: # (Each of T_total tokens visits K experts, but total work = T_total * K * (2*H*I*2)
12: # only if you count routing. The standard MoE FLOPs convention counts only the
13: # active per-token compute: T_total tokens * 2 * (2*I) * H. We follow that.)
14: flops_formula: "2 * T_total * H * (2 * I)"
15: 
16: # Bytes moved (approximate, lower bound):
17: #   read hidden (T_perm = T_total*K rows of H bf16) + read 2 weight matrices per
18: #   expert (E * H * 2*I bf16) + write output (T_perm rows of I bf16).
19: bytes_formula: "T_total*K*H*2 + E*H*(2*I)*2 + T_total*K*I*2"
20: 
21: tolerance:
22:   bfloat16: 0.02
23: 
24: # Forbidden ops -- agent must write the grouped GEMM + fused SwiGLU themselves.
25: # - torch.matmul / torch.bmm / F.linear: cuBLAS dispatch, defeats the point.
26: # - sonic_moe imports: vendor-call cheating; the SOTA is graded separately.
27: forbidden:
28:   - "torch.matmul"
29:   - "torch.bmm"
30:   - "torch.nn.functional.linear"
31:   - "F.linear"
32:   - "from sonic_moe"
33:   - "import son

Matrix multiply: (BLOCK_M, BLOCK_K) @ (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N) -> (BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N)\n        acc_gate += tl.dot(x.to(tl.float32), w_gate.to(tl.float32))\n        acc_up += tl.dot(x.to(tl.float32), w_up.to(tl.float32))\n    \n    # SwiGLU: silu(gate) * up\n    # silu(x) = x * sigmoid(x)\n    gate_silu = acc_gate * tl.sigmoid(acc_gate)\n    out = gate_silu * acc_up\n    \n    # Store output\n    out_ptr = output_ptr + (start + m_start) * I + n_start\n    tl.store(out_ptr + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)[:, None] * I + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)[None, :],\n             out.to(tl.bfloat16),\n             mask=(tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)[:, None] < m_size) & (tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)[None, :] < n_size))\n\n\nclass Model(nn.Module):\n    "', 'Up-projection of a top-K MoE FFN with fused SwiGLU (Triton kernel)."', '\n\n    def __init__(self, T_total: int, H: int, I: int, E: int, K: int):  # noqa: E741\n        super().__init__()\n        self.T_total = T_total\n        self.H = H\n        self.I = I\n        self.E = E\n        self.K = K\n        self.W_gate = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(E, H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16))\n        self.W_up = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(E, H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16))\n        nn.init.normal_(self.W_gate, std=0.02)\n        nn.init.normal_(self.W_up, std=0.02)\n        \n        # Block sizes - tuned for SM120\n        self.BLOCK_M = 128\n        self.BLOCK_N = 128\n        self.BLOCK_K = 32\n\n    def forward(\n        self,\n        hidden_states: torch.Tensor,   # (T_perm, H) bf16\n        expert_offsets: torch.Tensor,  # (E+1,) int32\n    ) -> torch.Tensor:\n        T_perm, H = hidden_states.shape\n        assert H == self.H\n        assert T_perm == self.T_total * self.K\n        \n        output = torch.empty(T_perm, self.I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=hidden_states.device)\n        \n        # Compute max M for grid\n        max_M = 0\n        for e in range(self.E):\n            start = int(expert_offsets[e].item())\n            end = int(expert_offsets[e + 1].item())\n            max_M = max(max_M, end - start)\n        \n        grid = (\n            self.E,\n            triton.cdiv(self.I, self.BLOCK_N),\n            triton.cdiv(max_M, self.BLOCK_M),\n        )\n        \n        grouped_gemm_swiglu_kernel[grid](\n            hidden_states,\n            self.W_gate,\n            self.W_up,\n            expert_offsets,\n            output,\n            T_perm, H, self.I, self.E,\n            self.BLOCK_M, self.BLOCK_N, self.BLOCK_K,\n        )\n        \n        return output\n\n\n# Module-level shape shims rewritten by check.py / benchmark.py per shape.\nT_total = 32768\nH = 4096\nI = 1536  # noqa: E741\nE = 128\nK = 8\n\n\ndef _build_routing(T_total: int, E: int, K: int, device: str = "cpu', 'torch.Tensor:\n    T_perm = T_total * K\n    base = T_perm // E\n    rem = T_perm - base * E\n    counts = torch.full((E,), base, dtype=torch.int32, device=device)\n    counts[:rem] += 1\n    offsets = torch.zeros(E + 1, dtype=torch.int32, device=device)\n    offsets[1:] = torch.cumsum(counts, dim=0)\n    return offsets\n\n\ndef get_inputs():\n    T_perm = T_total * K\n    hidden_states = torch.randn(T_perm, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1\n    expert_offsets = _build_routing(T_total, E, K)\n    return [hidden_states, expert_offsets]\n\n\ndef get_init_inputs():\n    return [T_total, H, I, E, K]']

Block sizes - tuned for SM120\n        self.BLOCK_M = 128\n        self.BLOCK_N = 128\n        self.BLOCK_K = 32\n\n    def forward(\n        self,\n        hidden_states: torch.Tensor,   # (T_perm, H) bf16\n        expert_offsets: torch.Tensor,  # (E+1,) int32\n    ) -> torch.Tensor:\n        T_perm, H = hidden_states.shape\n        assert H == self.H\n        assert T_perm == self.T_total * self.K\n\n        output = torch.empty(T_perm, self.I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=hidden_states.device)\n\n        # Load W_up tile: (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N)\n        w_up_ptr_e = W_up_ptr + expert_id * H * I + k_start * I + n_start\n        w_up = tl.load(\n            w_up_ptr_e + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)[:, None] * I + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)[None, :],\n            mask=(tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)[:, None] < k_size) & (tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)[None, :] < n_size_tile),\n            other=0.0\n        )\n\n        # Matrix multiply: (BLOCK_M, BLOCK_K) @ (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N) -> (BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N)\n        acc_gate += tl.dot(x.to(tl.float32), w_gate.to(tl.float32))\n        acc_up += tl.dot(x.to(tl.float32), w_up.to(tl.float32))\n\n    # SwiGLU: silu(gate) * up\n    # silu(x) = x * sigmoid(x)\n    gate_silu = acc_gate * tl.sigmoid(acc_gate)\n    out = gate_silu * acc_up\n\n    # Store output\n    out_ptr = output_ptr + (start + m_start) * I + n_start\n    tl.store(\n        out_ptr + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)[:, None] * I + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)[None, :],\n        out.to(tl.bfloat16),\n        mask=(tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)[:, None] < m_size_tile) & (tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)[None, :] < n_size_tile)\n    )\n\n\nclass Model(nn.Module):\n    """Up-projection of a top-K MoE FFN with fused SwiGLU.\n\n    Inputs at call time:\n      hidden_states:    (T_perm, H)  bf16, already permuted to expert order\n      expert_offsets:   (E+1,)       int32, prefix sums of token counts per expert\n                                       so expert e owns rows [offsets[e]:offsets[e+1]]\n                                       T_perm = T_total * K (each token visits K experts)\n\n    Output:\n      gated_up:         (T_perm, I)  bf16\n    """\n\n    def __init__(self, T_total: int, H: int, I: int, E: int, K: int):  # noqa: E741\n        super().__init__()\n        self.T_total = T_total\n        self.H = H\n        self.I = I\n        self.E = E\n        self.K = K\n        self.W_gate = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(E, H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16))\n        self.W_up = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(E, H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16))\n        nn.init.normal_(self.W_gate, std=0.02)\n        nn.init.normal_(self.W_up, std=0.02)\n\n        # Block sizes - tuned for SM120\n        self.BLOCK_M = 128\n        self.BLOCK_N = 128\n        self.BLOCK_K = 32\n\n    def forward(\n        self,\n        hidden_states: torch.Tensor,   # (T_perm, H) bf16\n        expert_offsets: torch.Tensor,  # (E+1,) int32\n    ) -> torch.Tensor:\n        T_perm, H = hidden_states.shape\n        assert H == self.H\n        assert T_perm == self.T_total * self.K\n\n        output = torch.empty(T_perm, self.I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=hidden_states.device)\n\n        # Compute max M for grid\n        max_M = 0\n        for e in range(self.E):\n            start = int(expert_offsets[e].item())\n            end = int(expert_offsets[e + 1].item())\n            max_M = max(max_M, end - start)\n\n        grid = (\n            self.E,\n            triton.cdiv(self.I, self.BLOCK_N),\n            triton.cdiv(max_M, self.BLOCK_M),\n        )\n\n        grouped_gemm_swiglu_kernel[grid](\n            hidden_states,\n            self.W_gate,\n            self.W_up,\n            expert_offsets,\n            output,\n            T_perm, H, self.I, self.E,\n            self.BLOCK_M, self.BLOCK_N, self.BLOCK_K,\n        )\n\n        return output\n\n\n# Module-level shape shims rewritten by check.py / benchmark.py per shape.\nT_total = 32768\nH = 4096\nI = 1536  # noqa: E741\nE = 128\nK = 8\n\n\ndef _build_routing(T_total: int, E: int, K: int, device: str = "cpu") -> torch.Tensor:\n    T_perm = T_total * K\n    base = T_perm // E\n    rem = T_perm - base * E\n    counts = torch.full((E,), base, dtype=torch.int32, device=device)\n    counts[:rem] += 1\n    offsets = torch.zeros(E + 1, dtype=torch.int32, device=device)\n    offsets[1:] = torch.cumsum(counts, dim=0)\n    return offsets\n\n\ndef get_inputs():\n    T_perm = T_total * K\n    hidden_states = torch.randn(T_perm, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1\n    expert_offsets = _build_routing(T_total, E, K)\n    return [hidden_states, expert_offsets]\n\n\ndef get_init_inputs():\n    return [T_total, H, I, E, K]\'\'\'\n\nwith open("/workspace/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu/solution.py", "w") as f:\n    f.write(content)\nprint("Done"]]']

self.E,\n            triton.cdiv(self.I, self.BLOCK_N),\n            triton.cdiv(max_M, self.BLOCK_M),\n        )\n\n        grouped_gemm_swiglu_kernel[grid](\n            hidden_states,\n            self.W_gate,\n            self.W_up,\n            expert_offsets,\n            output,\n            T_perm, H, self.I, self.E,\n            self.BLOCK_M, self.BLOCK_N, self.BLOCK_K,\n        )\n\n noqa: E741\n        super().__init__()\n        self.T_total = T_total\n        self.H = H\n        self.I = I\n        self.E = E\n        self.K = K\n        self.W_gate = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(E, H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16))\n        self.W_up = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(E, H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16))\n        nn.init.normal_(self.W_gate, std=0.02)\n        nn.init.normal_(self.W_up, std=0.02)\n\n        # Block sizes - tuned for SM120\n        self.BLOCK_M = 128\n        self.BLOCK_N = 128\n        self.BLOCK_K = 32\n\n    def forward(\n        self,\n        hidden_states: torch.Tensor,   # (T_perm, H) bf16\n        expert_offsets: torch.Tensor,  # (E+1,) int32\n    ) -> torch.Tensor:\n        T_perm, H = hidden_states.shape\n        assert H == self.H\n        assert T_perm == self.T_total * self.K\n\n        output = torch.empty(T_perm, self.I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=hidden_states.device)\n\n        # Compute max M for grid\n        max_M = 0\n        for e in range(self.E):\n            start = int(expert_offsets[e].item())\n            end = int(expert_offsets[e + 1].item())\n            max_M = max(max_M, end - start)\n\n        grid = (\n            self.E,\n            triton.cdiv(self.I, self.BLOCK_N),\n            triton.cdiv(max_M, self.BLOCK_M),\n        )\n\n        grouped_gemm_swiglu_kernel[grid](\n            hidden_states,\n            self.W_gate,\n            self.W_up,\n            expert_offsets,\n            output,\n            T_perm, H, self.I, self.E,\n            self.BLOCK_M, self.BLOCK_N, self.BLOCK_K,\n        )\n\n        return output\n\n\n# Module-level shape shims rewritten by check.py / benchmark.py per shape.\nT_total = 32768\nH = 4096\nI = 1536  # noqa: E741\nE = 128\nK = 8\n\n\ndef _build_routing(T_total: int, E: int, K: int, device: str = "cpu") -> torch.Tensor:\n    T_perm = T_total * K\n    base = T_perm // E\n    rem = T_perm - base * E\n    counts = torch.full((E,), base, dtype=torch.int32, device=device)\n    counts[:rem] += 1\n    offsets = torch.zeros(E + 1, dtype=torch.int32, device=device)\n    offsets[1:] = torch.cumsum(counts, dim=0)\n    return offsets\n\n\ndef get_inputs():\n    T_perm = T_total * K\n    hidden_states = torch.randn(T_perm, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1\n    expert_offsets = _build_routing(T_total, E, K)\n    return [hidden_states, expert_offsets]\n\n\ndef get_init_inputs():\n    return [T_total, H, I, E, K]\'\'\'\n\nwith open("/workspace/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu/solution.py", "w") as f:\n    f.write(content)\nprint("Done"]]']+['None] * H + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)[None, :],\n            mask=(tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)[:, None] < m_size_tile) & (tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)[None, :] < k_size),\n            other=0.0\n        )\n\n        w_gate_ptr_e = W_gate_ptr + expert_id * H * I + k_start * I + n_start\n        w_gate = tl.load(\n            w_gate_ptr_e + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)[:, None] * I + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)[None, :],\n            mask=(tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)[:, None] < k_size) & (tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)[None, :] < n_size_tile),\n            other=0.0\n        )\n\n        w_up_ptr_e = W_up_ptr + expert_id * H * I + k_start * I + n_start\n        w_up = tl.load(\n            w_up_ptr_e + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)[:, None] * I + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)[None, :],\n            mask=(tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)[:, None] < k_size) & (tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)[None, :] < n_size_tile),\n            other=0.0\n        )\n\n        acc_gate += tl.dot(x.to(tl.float32), w_gate.to(tl.float32))\n        acc_up += tl.dot(x.to(tl.float32), w_up.to(tl.float32))\n\n    gate_si
